_loader.use('jquery, mediav', function () {
    if (!window.MediavAds) {
        return;
    }

    var query = 'python编程';
    var showId = {
        high: 'f9CPx3', // 高相关性
        middle: 'vmoZZE' // 中相关性
    }

    // 获取高相关性广告 获取不到则获取中相关性广告
    function getMediavHighRel() {
        var mediavHighRel = new MediavAds({
            $dom: $('#mohe-kzx_top'),   // 必传: 包含广告内容的容器dom
            itemWrap: '.mh-ad',            // 必传: 每条广告的外层容器
            apiUrl: {                     // 选填：广告请求地址
                http: 'http://show.g.mediav.com/s',
                https: 'https://show-g.mediav.com/s?scheme=https'
            },
            params: {                     // 广告请求接口参数
                showid: showId.high,         // 异步获取数据必传（由商业化提供 ），同步传递数据不传
                queryword: query,  // 选填：做相关性广告传，做不相关性广告则不需要
                impct: 1,  // 选填： 默认为2（请求两条广告数据）
                reqtimes: 1, // 选填：传递数字值，如果传值，每请求一次数据加1
            },
            scrollNamespace: '.haosou.mediavXXL',
            beforeSend: function() {
                monitorLog(showId.high);
            },
            successCallback: function (data) { // 获取mediav数据成功后的回调
                if(data && data.ads && data.ads.length) {
                    renderItem(data);
                } else {
                    getMediavMiddleRel();
                }
            },
            errorCallback: function (errorMsg) {
                getMediavMiddleRel();
            },
            noDataCallback: function () {
                getMediavMiddleRel();
            },
        });
    }

    // 获取中相关性广告
    function getMediavMiddleRel() {
        return new MediavAds({
            $dom: $('#mohe-kzx_top'),   // 必传: 包含广告内容的容器dom
            itemWrap: '.mh-ad',            // 必传: 每条广告的外层容器
            apiUrl: {                     // 选填：广告请求地址， 默认值为http://show.3.mediav.com/s和 https://show-3.mediav.com/s?scheme=https
                http: 'http://show.g.mediav.com/s',
                https: 'https://show-g.mediav.com/s?scheme=https'
            },
            params: {                     // 广告请求接口参数
                showid: showId.middle,         // 异步获取数据必传（由商业化提供 ），同步传递数据不传
                queryword: query,  // 选填：做相关性广告传，做不相关性广告则不需要
                impct: 1,  // 选填： 默认为2（请求两条广告数据）
                reqtimes: 1, // 选填：传递数字值，如果传值，每请求一次数据加1
            },
            scrollNamespace: '.haosou.mediavXXL',
            beforeSend: function() {
                monitorLog(showId.middle);
            },
            successCallback: function (data) { // 获取mediav数据成功后的回调
                if(data && data.ads && data.ads.length) {
                    renderItem(data);
                }
            },
        });
    }


    function renderItem(data) {
        var ad = data.ads[0];
        var $list = $('#mohe-kzx_top .js-mh-list');
        var img = ad.img || ad.assets[0].img;
        var html = '<li><a class="js-mh-item mh-ad" title="'+ ad.title + '" href="' + ad.curl + '" target="_blank" data-md={"p":"mediav"} data-index="0">\
                        <div class="g-figure-layout-v">\
                            <div class="g-img-wrap">\
                                <div class="g-img-inner g-img-def">\
                                    <img src="'+ img + '" alt="' + ad.title + '" class="g-img">\
                                    <div class="g-img-mask"></div>\
                                    <span class="mh-ad-tip"></span>\
                                </div>\
                            </div>\
                        </div>\
                        <div class="g-figure-caption g-ellipsis2">' + ad.title + '</div>\
                    </a></li>'
        $list.find('.js-mh-item').eq(3).remove();
        $list.find('.js-mh-item').eq(2).after(html);

        // 模拟展现打点
        window.PageLine && PageLine.fill && PageLine.fill({
            'cat': 'kzx_top-mediav-moni'
        });
    }
    setTimeout(function(){
        getMediavHighRel();
    }, 1000);

    /**
     * 模拟打点
     * @params showid 广告唯一标识
     */
    function monitorLog(showid) {
        window.PageLine && PageLine.fill && PageLine.fill({
            'cat': 'kzx_top-mediav-request-moni',
            'md-b': showid,
            'md-p': '6'
        });
    }
});

        $(".e-icon-drip").click(function (e) {

            e.stopPropagation();
            $("#eLandpage").remove();

        function imgScaling (imgWidth, imgHeight, containerWidth, containerHeight) {
            var containerRatio = containerWidth / containerHeight
            var imgRatio = imgWidth / imgHeight
            if (imgRatio > containerRatio) {
                imgWidth = containerWidth
                imgHeight = imgWidth / imgRatio
            } else {
                imgHeight = containerHeight
                imgWidth = imgHeight * imgRatio
            }
            var imgMargin = ((containerHeight - imgHeight) / 2) + 'px ' + ((containerWidth - imgWidth) / 2) + 'px'
            return {width: imgWidth, height: imgHeight, margin: imgMargin}
        }
        function drawImg (imgObj, containerWidth, containerHeight) {
            var $this = $(imgObj)
            var imgWidth = $this.width()
            var imgHeight = $this.height()
            var newImgAttr = imgScaling(imgWidth, imgHeight, containerWidth, containerHeight)
            $this.attr({'width': newImgAttr.width, 'height': newImgAttr.height})
            $this.css('margin', newImgAttr.margin)
        }
    });
</script>

    //实地认证
    _loader.use("jquery", function () {
        window.cer = new Array();
        var t2;
        function mouseDirection(wrap, ev, fn) {
            var w = wrap.offsetWidth;
            var h = wrap.offsetHeight;
            var toTop = wrap.getBoundingClientRect().top + document.documentElement.scrollTop;
            var x = (ev.pageX - wrap.getBoundingClientRect().left - (w / 2)) * (w > h ? (h / w) : 1);
            var y = (ev.pageY - toTop - (h / 2)) * (h > w ? (w / h) : 1);
            var direction = Math.round((((Math.atan2(y, x) * 180 / Math.PI) + 180) / 90) + 3) % 4;
            if(fn) {
                fn(direction);
            }
        }
        var node = null;
        $(".certification-tag ").on("mouseenter", function(){
            if($("body>.certification").length > 0) {
                $("body>.certification").remove();
            }
            var offsetLeft = 0;
            if ($(this).text() == "") {
                offsetLeft = 120;
            } else {
                offsetLeft = 50;
            }
            $(this).next().find(".arrow").css("left", $(this).offset().left - offsetLeft + "px");
            var point = $(this).offset();
            node = $(this).next(".certification").clone();
            $("body").append(node);
            node.css("top", point.top + 25 + "px");
            node.show();

            var index = $(".certification-tag").index(this);

            t2 = setTimeout(function(){
                if (!window.cer[index]){
                    var imgId_cer="e_log_cer"+(new Date).getTime();
                    var img_cer=new Image;
                    window[imgId_cer]=img_cer;
                    img_cer.onload=img_cer.onerror=function(){window[imgId_cer]=null};
                    img_cer.src=node.attr("e-url");
                }
                window.cer[index] = true;
            },500)

            node.on("mouseleave", function(){
                clearTimeout(t2);
                node.remove();
            });
        }).on("mouseleave", function(e){
            mouseDirection(this, e, function(direct){
                if (direct != 2) {
                    clearTimeout(t2);
                    node.remove();
                }
            })
        });
    });
</script>
